"""

class Config:
    """Configuration for training DenseNet-121 and EfficientNet-B0"""

    # ==================== PATHS ====================
    PROJECT_ROOT = Path('/content/drive/MyDrive/chest-xray-project')
    DATA_ROOT = PROJECT_ROOT / 'datasets'
    OUTPUT_DIR = PROJECT_ROOT / 'outputs'
    MODELS_DIR = OUTPUT_DIR / 'models'
    RESULTS_DIR = OUTPUT_DIR / 'results'
    FIGURES_DIR = OUTPUT_DIR / 'figures'

    # MIMIC-CXR paths
    MIMIC_ROOT = DATA_ROOT / 'mimic-cxr'
    MIMIC_FILES = MIMIC_ROOT / 'files'
    MIMIC_TRAIN_CSV = DATA_ROOT / 'mimic_train.csv'
    MIMIC_VAL_CSV = DATA_ROOT / 'mimic_val.csv'
    MIMIC_TEST_CSV = DATA_ROOT / 'mimic_test.csv'

    # CheXpert paths
    CHEXPERT_ROOT = DATA_ROOT / 'chexpert'
    CHEXPERT_VAL_CSV = DATA_ROOT / 'chexpert_val.csv'

    # ==================== TRAINING HYPERPARAMETERS ====================
    BATCH_SIZE = 32
    NUM_EPOCHS = 25
    LEARNING_RATE = 1e-4
    WEIGHT_DECAY = 1e-4
    EARLY_STOPPING_PATIENCE = 5

    # ==================== MODEL SETTINGS ====================
    NUM_CLASSES = 14
    IMG_SIZE = 224
    USE_AMP = True  # Automatic Mixed Precision
    NUM_WORKERS = 4
    SEED = 42

    # ==================== PATHOLOGIES (14 total) ====================
    PATHOLOGIES = [
        'Atelectasis',
        'Cardiomegaly',
        'Consolidation',
        'Edema',
        'Pleural Effusion',
        'Pneumonia',
        'Pneumothorax',
        'No Finding',
        'Enlarged Cardiomediastinum',
        'Lung Opacity',
        'Lung Lesion',
        'Fracture',
        'Support Devices',
        'Pleural Other'
    ]

    # ==================== ARCHITECTURES TO TRAIN ====================
    ARCHITECTURES = ['densenet121', 'efficientnet_b0']

# Create output directories
for dir_path in [Config.MODELS_DIR, Config.RESULTS_DIR, Config.FIGURES_DIR]:
    dir_path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

# Set random seeds for reproducibility
def set_seed(seed=42):
    torch.manual_seed(seed)
    torch.cuda.manual_seed_all(seed)
    np.random.seed(seed)
    torch.backends.cudnn.deterministic = True
    torch.backends.cudnn.benchmark = False

set_seed(Config.SEED)

# Check device
device = torch.device('cuda' if torch.cuda.is_available() else 'cpu')
if torch.cuda.is_available():
    print(f" GPU: {torch.cuda.get_device_name(0)}")
    print(f" GPU Memory: {torch.cuda.get_device_properties(0).total_memory / 1e9:.1f} GB")
else:
    print(" No GPU available - using CPU")

print(f"\n Configuration complete")
print(f" Output directories created")
print(f" Random seed set: {Config.SEED}\n")

# ===== STEP 4: DATASET CLASS =====

class ChestXRayDataset(Dataset):
    """Dataset that takes CSV path (not DataFrame)"""

    def __init__(self, csv_path, img_root, transform=None):
        self.df = pd.read_csv(csv_path)
        self.img_root = Path(img_root)
        self.transform = transform
        self.pathologies = Config.PATHOLOGY_LABELS

    def __len__(self):
        return len(self.df)

    def __getitem__(self, idx):
        row = self.df.iloc[idx]

        # MIMIC-CXR path format
        subject_id = row['subject_id']
        study_id = row['study_id']
        dicom_id = row['dicom_id']
        img_path = self.img_root / f'p{str(subject_id)[:2]}' / f'p{subject_id}' / f's{study_id}' / f'{dicom_id}.jpg'

        try:
            img = Image.open(img_path).convert('RGB')
        except:
            img = Image.new('RGB', (Config.IMG_SIZE, Config.IMG_SIZE))

        if self.transform:
            img = self.transform(img)

        labels = []
        for pathology in self.pathologies:
            if pathology in row:
                label = row[pathology]
                if pd.isna(label) or label == -1.0:
                    labels.append(-1.0)
                else:
                    labels.append(float(label))
            else:
                labels.append(-1.0)

        return img, torch.tensor(labels, dtype=torch.float32)

print("ChestXRayDataset class defined")

ChestXRayDataset class defined

class ChestXRayDataset(Dataset):
    """
    Dataset for chest X-ray images with multi-label classification
    Handles uncertain labels (-1, NaN) with masking
    """

    def __init__(self, csv_path, img_root, transform=None):
        self.df = pd.read_csv(csv_path)
        self.img_root = Path(img_root)
        self.transform = transform
        self.pathologies = Config.PATHOLOGIES  # Fixed: was PATHOLOGY_LABELS

    def __len__(self):
        return len(self.df)

    def __getitem__(self, idx):
        row = self.df.iloc[idx]

        # Construct image path
        if 'path' in row:
            img_path = self.img_root / row['path']
        else:
            subject_id = row['subject_id']
            study_id = row['study_id']
            dicom_id = row['dicom_id']
            img_path = self.img_root / f'p{str(subject_id)[:2]}' / f'p{subject_id}' / f's{study_id}' / f'{dicom_id}.jpg'

        try:
            img = Image.open(img_path).convert('RGB')
        except:
            img = Image.new('RGB', (Config.IMG_SIZE, Config.IMG_SIZE))

        if self.transform:
            img = self.transform(img)

        labels = []
        for pathology in self.pathologies:
            if pathology in row:
                label = row[pathology]
                if pd.isna(label) or label == -1.0:
                    labels.append(-1.0)
                else:
                    labels.append(float(label))
            else:
                labels.append(-1.0)

        return img, torch.tensor(labels, dtype=torch.float32)

In[]:
class ChestXRayDataset(Dataset):
    def __init__(self, csv_path, img_root, transform=None):
        self.df = pd.read_csv(csv_path)
        self.img_root = Path(img_root)
        self.transform = transform
        self.pathologies = Config.PATHOLOGIES

        # Fix CheXpert: rename 'Path' to 'path' if needed
        if 'Path' in self.df.columns and 'path' not in self.df.columns:
            self.df['path'] = self.df['Path'].apply(
                lambda x: x.replace('CheXpert-v1.0/valid/', '') if isinstance(x, str) else x
            )

    def __len__(self):
        return len(self.df)

    def __getitem__(self, idx):
        row = self.df.iloc[idx]

        # Check for path column (CheXpert format)
        if 'path' in row:
            img_path = self.img_root / row['path']
        else:
            # MIMIC-CXR format
            subject_id = row['subject_id']
            study_id = row['study_id']
            dicom_id = row['dicom_id']
            img_path = self.img_root / f'p{str(subject_id)[:2]}' / f'p{subject_id}' / f's{study_id}' / f'{dicom_id}.jpg'

        try:
            img = Image.open(img_path).convert('RGB')
        except:
            img = Image.new('RGB', (Config.IMG_SIZE, Config.IMG_SIZE))

        if self.transform:
            img = self.transform(img)

        labels = []
        for pathology in self.pathologies:
            if pathology in row:
                label = row[pathology]
                if pd.isna(label) or label == -1.0:
                    labels.append(-1.0)
                else:
                    labels.append(float(label))
            else:
                labels.append(-1.0)

        return img, torch.tensor(labels, dtype=torch.float32)

print(" ChestXRayDataset class updated (handles CheXpert 'Path' column)")

"""
CHUNK 6: Data Augmentation and Preprocessing Transforms
"""

def get_train_transforms():
    """
    Training transforms with data augmentation
    """
    return transforms.Compose([
        transforms.Resize(256),
        transforms.RandomCrop(Config.IMG_SIZE),
        transforms.RandomHorizontalFlip(p=0.5),
        transforms.RandomRotation(degrees=10),
        transforms.ColorJitter(brightness=0.2, contrast=0.2),
        transforms.ToTensor(),
        transforms.Normalize(mean=[0.485, 0.456, 0.406],
                           std=[0.229, 0.224, 0.225])
    ])

def get_val_transforms():
    """
    Validation/test transforms (no augmentation)
    """
    return transforms.Compose([
        transforms.Resize(256),
        transforms.CenterCrop(Config.IMG_SIZE),
        transforms.ToTensor(),
        transforms.Normalize(mean=[0.485, 0.456, 0.406],
                           std=[0.229, 0.224, 0.225])
    ])

print(" Data transforms defined")
print("  - Training: RandomCrop, HorizontalFlip, Rotation, ColorJitter")
print("  - Validation: CenterCrop only\n")

 Data transforms defined
  - Training: RandomCrop, HorizontalFlip, Rotation, ColorJitter
  - Validation: CenterCrop only

"""
CHUNK 7: Model Architecture Definition
"""

class ChestXRayClassifier(nn.Module):
    """
    Multi-label chest X-ray classifier
    Supports: ResNet-50, DenseNet-121, EfficientNet-B0
    """

    def __init__(self, architecture='densenet121', num_classes=14, pretrained=True):
        super().__init__()
        self.architecture = architecture

        # Load backbone
        if architecture == 'resnet50':
            self.backbone = models.resnet50(pretrained=pretrained)
            num_features = self.backbone.fc.in_features
            self.backbone.fc = nn.Identity()

        elif architecture == 'densenet121':
            self.backbone = models.densenet121(pretrained=pretrained)
            num_features = self.backbone.classifier.in_features
            self.backbone.classifier = nn.Identity()

        elif architecture == 'efficientnet_b0':
            self.backbone = timm.create_model('efficientnet_b0', pretrained=pretrained)
            num_features = self.backbone.classifier.in_features
            self.backbone.classifier = nn.Identity()

        else:
            raise ValueError(f"Unknown architecture: {architecture}")

        # Classification head
        self.classifier = nn.Sequential(
            nn.Dropout(0.2),
            nn.Linear(num_features, num_classes)
        )

    def forward(self, x):
        features = self.backbone(x)
        logits = self.classifier(features)
        return logits

print(" ChestXRayClassifier class defined")
print("  Supported architectures: ResNet-50, DenseNet-121, EfficientNet-B0\n")

 ChestXRayClassifier class defined
  Supported architectures: ResNet-50, DenseNet-121, EfficientNet-B0

  • 8: Masked BCE Loss Function
In[]:
"""
CHUNK 8: Masked BCE Loss Function
Handles uncertain labels (-1) by masking them out
"""

class MaskedBCEWithLogitsLoss(nn.Module):
    """
    Binary Cross-Entropy loss that ignores uncertain labels (-1)
    Uses pos_weight for class imbalance handling
    """

    def __init__(self, pos_weight=None):
        super().__init__()
        self.pos_weight = pos_weight
        self.bce = nn.BCEWithLogitsLoss(reduction='none', pos_weight=pos_weight)

    def forward(self, logits, targets):
        """
        Args:
            logits: (batch_size, num_classes) - raw model outputs
            targets: (batch_size, num_classes) - labels with -1 for uncertain

        Returns:
            loss: Scalar loss value (averaged over certain labels only)
        """
        # Create mask: 1 where certain (0 or 1), 0 where uncertain (-1)
        mask = (targets != -1).float()

        # Replace -1 with 0 for BCE computation (won't affect loss due to mask)
        targets_masked = targets.clone()
        targets_masked[targets == -1] = 0

        # Compute BCE loss
        loss = self.bce(logits, targets_masked)

        # Apply mask and compute average (only over certain labels)
        loss = (loss * mask).sum() / (mask.sum() + 1e-8)

        return loss

print(" MaskedBCEWithLogitsLoss class defined")
print("  - Masks out uncertain labels (-1)")
print("  - Supports positive class weights for imbalance\n")

 MaskedBCEWithLogitsLoss class defined
  - Masks out uncertain labels (-1)
  - Supports positive class weights for imbalance

"""
CHUNK 9: Training and Validation Functions
"""

def compute_pos_weights(train_loader):
    """
    Compute positive class weights for handling class imbalance
    Returns neg/pos ratio for each pathology
    """
    print("Computing class weights for imbalanced data...\n")

    pos_counts = torch.zeros(Config.NUM_CLASSES)
    neg_counts = torch.zeros(Config.NUM_CLASSES)

    for _, labels in tqdm(train_loader, desc="Computing weights"):
        for i in range(Config.NUM_CLASSES):
            mask = labels[:, i] != -1  # Only count certain labels
            pos_counts[i] += (labels[:, i][mask] == 1).sum()
            neg_counts[i] += (labels[:, i][mask] == 0).sum()

    # Compute neg/pos ratio
    pos_weights = neg_counts / (pos_counts + 1e-8)

    print("\nClass Weights (neg/pos ratio):")
    print(f"{'Pathology':<35s} {'Weight':>8s} {'Pos':>10s} {'Neg':>10s}")
    print("-" * 70)
    for i, pathology in enumerate(Config.PATHOLOGIES):
        print(f"{pathology:<35s} {pos_weights[i]:8.2f} {int(pos_counts[i]):10d} {int(neg_counts[i]):10d}")
    print()

    return pos_weights


def train_epoch(model, train_loader, criterion, optimizer, scaler, device):
    """
    Train model for one epoch
    """
    model.train()
    running_loss = 0.0

    progress_bar = tqdm(train_loader, desc="Training")
    for images, labels in progress_bar:
        images = images.to(device)
        labels = labels.to(device)

        optimizer.zero_grad()

        # Mixed precision training
        if Config.USE_AMP:
            with autocast():
                logits = model(images)
                loss = criterion(logits, labels)

            scaler.scale(loss).backward()
            scaler.unscale_(optimizer)
            torch.nn.utils.clip_grad_norm_(model.parameters(), 1.0)
            scaler.step(optimizer)
            scaler.update()
        else:
            logits = model(images)
            loss = criterion(logits, labels)
            loss.backward()
            torch.nn.utils.clip_grad_norm_(model.parameters(), 1.0)
            optimizer.step()

        running_loss += loss.item()
        progress_bar.set_postfix({'loss': f'{loss.item():.4f}'})

    return running_loss / len(train_loader)


def validate_epoch(model, val_loader, criterion, device):
    """
    Validate model for one epoch
    """
    model.eval()
    running_loss = 0.0

    with torch.no_grad():
        for images, labels in tqdm(val_loader, desc="Validation"):
            images = images.to(device)
            labels = labels.to(device)

            logits = model(images)
            loss = criterion(logits, labels)

            running_loss += loss.item()

    return running_loss / len(val_loader)

print(" Training functions defined")
print("  - compute_pos_weights()")
print("  - train_epoch()")
print("  - validate_epoch()\n")

 Training functions defined
  - compute_pos_weights()
  - train_epoch()
  - validate_epoch()

"""
CHUNK 10: Model Evaluation and Metrics Computation
"""

def evaluate_model(model, dataloader, device):
    """
    Evaluate model and compute metrics for all pathologies

    Returns:
        metrics: Dict with AUC, AUPRC, F1 for each pathology
    """
    model.eval()

    all_logits = []
    all_labels = []

    # Collect predictions
    with torch.no_grad():
        for images, labels in tqdm(dataloader, desc="Evaluating"):
            images = images.to(device)
            logits = model(images)

            all_logits.append(logits.cpu())
            all_labels.append(labels.cpu())

    # Concatenate all batches
    all_logits = torch.cat(all_logits, dim=0)
    all_labels = torch.cat(all_labels, dim=0)
    all_probs = torch.sigmoid(all_logits)

    # Compute metrics per pathology
    metrics = {}

    for i, pathology in enumerate(Config.PATHOLOGIES):
        # Only evaluate on certain labels
        mask = all_labels[:, i] != -1

        if mask.sum() == 0:
            continue

        y_true = all_labels[mask, i].numpy()
        y_prob = all_probs[mask, i].numpy()
        y_pred = (y_prob >= 0.5).astype(int)

        # Skip if only one class present
        if len(np.unique(y_true)) < 2:
            continue

        try:
            auc = roc_auc_score(y_true, y_prob)
            auprc = average_precision_score(y_true, y_prob)
            f1 = f1_score(y_true, y_pred, zero_division=0)

            metrics[pathology] = {
                'auc': auc,
                'auprc': auprc,
                'f1': f1,
                'n': mask.sum().item()
            }
        except Exception as e:
            # Skip pathologies with errors
            pass

    return metrics

print(" Evaluation function defined")
print("  - Computes AUC, AUPRC, F1 per pathology")
print("  - Handles uncertain labels with masking\n")

 Evaluation function defined
  - Computes AUC, AUPRC, F1 per pathology
  - Handles uncertain labels with masking

"""
CHUNK 11: Visualization Functions for Training Curves
"""

def plot_training_curves(history, architecture):
    """
    Plot and save training curves (loss and learning rate)
    """
    fig, axes = plt.subplots(1, 2, figsize=(14, 5))

    epochs = range(1, len(history['train_loss']) + 1)

    # Loss curves
    axes[0].plot(epochs, history['train_loss'], 'b-', label='Train Loss', linewidth=2)
    axes[0].plot(epochs, history['val_loss'], 'r-', label='Val Loss', linewidth=2)
    axes[0].set_xlabel('Epoch', fontsize=12)
    axes[0].set_ylabel('Loss', fontsize=12)
    axes[0].set_title(f'{architecture.upper()} - Training Curves', fontsize=14, fontweight='bold')
    axes[0].legend(fontsize=11)
    axes[0].grid(True, alpha=0.3)

    # Learning rate schedule
    axes[1].plot(epochs, history['lr'], 'g-', linewidth=2)
    axes[1].set_xlabel('Epoch', fontsize=12)
    axes[1].set_ylabel('Learning Rate', fontsize=12)
    axes[1].set_title('Learning Rate Schedule', fontsize=14, fontweight='bold')
    axes[1].grid(True, alpha=0.3)
    axes[1].set_yscale('log')

    plt.tight_layout()

    # Save figure
    save_path = Config.FIGURES_DIR / f'{architecture}_training_curves.png'
    plt.savefig(save_path, dpi=300, bbox_inches='tight')
    plt.close()

    print(f"   Training curves saved: {save_path}")

print(" Visualization function defined")
print("  - plot_training_curves()\n")

 Visualization function defined
  - plot_training_curves()

"""
CHUNK 12: Main Training Pipeline for One Architecture
"""

def train_model(architecture, train_loader, val_loader, device, pos_weights=None):
    """
    Complete training pipeline for one architecture

    Args:
        architecture: 'densenet121' or 'efficientnet_b0'
        train_loader: Training data loader
        val_loader: Validation data loader
        device: torch device (cuda/cpu)
        pos_weights: Positive class weights for imbalance

    Returns:
        model: Trained model
        history: Training history (losses, lr)
    """

    print(f"\n{'='*80}")
    print(f" TRAINING {architecture.upper()}")
    print(f"{'='*80}\n")

    start_time = time.time()

    # Initialize model
    model = ChestXRayClassifier(
        architecture=architecture,
        num_classes=Config.NUM_CLASSES,
        pretrained=True
    )
    model = model.to(device)

    # Count parameters
    total_params = sum(p.numel() for p in model.parameters())
    trainable_params = sum(p.numel() for p in model.parameters() if p.requires_grad)

    print(f"Model: {architecture}")
    print(f"  Total parameters:     {total_params:,}")
    print(f"  Trainable parameters: {trainable_params:,}\n")

    # Loss function with class weights
    if pos_weights is not None:
        pos_weights_tensor = pos_weights.to(device)
        criterion = MaskedBCEWithLogitsLoss(pos_weight=pos_weights_tensor)
        print(" Using weighted BCE loss for class imbalance")
    else:
        criterion = MaskedBCEWithLogitsLoss()
        print(" Using standard BCE loss")

    # Optimizer and scheduler
    optimizer = optim.AdamW(
        model.parameters(),
        lr=Config.LEARNING_RATE,
        weight_decay=Config.WEIGHT_DECAY
    )
    scheduler = optim.lr_scheduler.CosineAnnealingLR(
        optimizer,
        T_max=Config.NUM_EPOCHS
    )

    print(f" Optimizer: AdamW (lr={Config.LEARNING_RATE}, wd={Config.WEIGHT_DECAY})")
    print(f" Scheduler: CosineAnnealingLR (T_max={Config.NUM_EPOCHS})")

    # AMP scaler for mixed precision
    scaler = GradScaler() if Config.USE_AMP else None
    if Config.USE_AMP:
        print(" Mixed precision training enabled (AMP)")

    # Training history
    history = {
        'train_loss': [],
        'val_loss': [],
        'lr': []
    }

    best_val_loss = float('inf')
    epochs_no_improve = 0
    best_epoch = 0

    print(f"\nStarting training for up to {Config.NUM_EPOCHS} epochs...")
    print(f"Early stopping patience: {Config.EARLY_STOPPING_PATIENCE} epochs\n")

    # ==================== TRAINING LOOP ====================
    for epoch in range(1, Config.NUM_EPOCHS + 1):
        print(f"\n{'='*80}")
        print(f" Epoch {epoch}/{Config.NUM_EPOCHS}")
        print(f"{'='*80}\n")

        epoch_start = time.time()

        # Train
        train_loss = train_epoch(model, train_loader, criterion, optimizer, scaler, device)

        # Validate
        val_loss = validate_epoch(model, val_loader, criterion, device)

        # Update learning rate
        scheduler.step()
        current_lr = optimizer.param_groups[0]['lr']

        # Save history
        history['train_loss'].append(train_loss)
        history['val_loss'].append(val_loss)
        history['lr'].append(current_lr)

        epoch_time = time.time() - epoch_start

        # Print epoch summary
        print(f"\nEpoch {epoch} Summary:")
        print(f"  Train Loss: {train_loss:.4f}")
        print(f"  Val Loss:   {val_loss:.4f}")
        print(f"  LR:         {current_lr:.2e}")
        print(f"  Time:       {epoch_time/60:.1f} min")

        # Save best model
        if val_loss < best_val_loss:
            best_val_loss = val_loss
            best_epoch = epoch
            epochs_no_improve = 0

            model_path = Config.MODELS_DIR / f'{architecture}_best.pth'
            torch.save(model.state_dict(), model_path)
            print(f"   New best model saved (epoch {epoch})")
        else:
            epochs_no_improve += 1
            print(f"  No improvement for {epochs_no_improve} epoch(s)")

        # Early stopping
        if epochs_no_improve >= Config.EARLY_STOPPING_PATIENCE:
            print(f"\n Early stopping triggered at epoch {epoch}")
            print(f"  Best epoch: {best_epoch}")
            print(f"  Best val loss: {best_val_loss:.4f}")
            break

    # Training complete
    total_time = time.time() - start_time

    print(f"\n{'='*80}")
    print(f" TRAINING COMPLETE")
    print(f"{'='*80}")
    print(f"  Total time:     {total_time/3600:.2f} hours")
    print(f"  Best epoch:     {best_epoch}")
    print(f"  Best val loss:  {best_val_loss:.4f}\n")

    # Load best model
    print(f"Loading best model from epoch {best_epoch}...")
    model.load_state_dict(torch.load(Config.MODELS_DIR / f'{architecture}_best.pth'))
    print(" Best model loaded\n")

    # Plot training curves
    plot_training_curves(history, architecture)

    return model, history

print(" Main training pipeline defined")
print("  - train_model() function ready\n")

  - train_model() function ready

"""
CHUNK 13: Cross-Institutional Validation Function
Evaluates model on both MIMIC-CXR (internal) and CheXpert (external)
"""

def cross_institutional_validation(model, architecture, test_loader, chexpert_loader, device):
    """
    Evaluate model on internal and external test sets

    Args:
        model: Trained model
        architecture: Model architecture name
        test_loader: MIMIC-CXR test loader
        chexpert_loader: CheXpert validation loader
        device: torch device

    Returns:
        results: Dictionary with all evaluation results
    """

    print(f"\n{'='*80}")
    print(f" CROSS-INSTITUTIONAL VALIDATION - {architecture.upper()}")
    print(f"{'='*80}\n")

    # ==================== INTERNAL VALIDATION (MIMIC-CXR) ====================
    print("-" * 80)
    print(" INTERNAL VALIDATION (MIMIC-CXR Test Set)")
    print("-" * 80)
    print()

    mimic_metrics = evaluate_model(model, test_loader, device)

    # Print MIMIC results
    print(f"\n{'='*80}")
    print(" MIMIC-CXR TEST RESULTS")
    print(f"{'='*80}\n")

    mimic_aucs = [m['auc'] for m in mimic_metrics.values()]
    mimic_auprcs = [m['auprc'] for m in mimic_metrics.values()]
    mimic_f1s = [m['f1'] for m in mimic_metrics.values()]

    print("Average Metrics:")
    print(f"  AUC:   {np.mean(mimic_aucs):.4f}")
    print(f"  AUPRC: {np.mean(mimic_auprcs):.4f}")
    print(f"  F1:    {np.mean(mimic_f1s):.4f}\n")

    print("Per-Pathology Metrics:")
    print(f"{'Pathology':<35s} {'AUC':>7s} {'AUPRC':>7s} {'F1':>7s} {'N':>8s}")
    print("-" * 80)
    for pathology in Config.PATHOLOGIES:
        if pathology in mimic_metrics:
            m = mimic_metrics[pathology]
            print(f"{pathology:<35s} {m['auc']:7.4f} {m['auprc']:7.4f} {m['f1']:7.4f} {m['n']:8d}")

    # ==================== EXTERNAL VALIDATION (CheXpert) ====================
    print(f"\n{'-'*80}")
    print(" EXTERNAL VALIDATION (CheXpert)")
    print("-" * 80)
    print("Zero-shot evaluation (no target-domain fine-tuning)\n")

    chexpert_metrics = evaluate_model(model, chexpert_loader, device)

    # Print CheXpert results
    print(f"\n{'='*80}")
    print(" CHEXPERT RESULTS")
    print(f"{'='*80}\n")

    chexpert_aucs = [m['auc'] for m in chexpert_metrics.values()]
    chexpert_auprcs = [m['auprc'] for m in chexpert_metrics.values()]
    chexpert_f1s = [m['f1'] for m in chexpert_metrics.values()]

    print("Average Metrics:")
    print(f"  AUC:   {np.mean(chexpert_aucs):.4f}")
    print(f"  AUPRC: {np.mean(chexpert_auprcs):.4f}")
    print(f"  F1:    {np.mean(chexpert_f1s):.4f}\n")

    print("Per-Pathology Metrics:")
    print(f"{'Pathology':<35s} {'AUC':>7s} {'AUPRC':>7s} {'F1':>7s} {'N':>8s}")
    print("-" * 80)
    for pathology in Config.PATHOLOGIES:
        if pathology in chexpert_metrics:
            m = chexpert_metrics[pathology]
            print(f"{pathology:<35s} {m['auc']:7.4f} {m['auprc']:7.4f} {m['f1']:7.4f} {m['n']:8d}")

    # ==================== GENERALIZATION ANALYSIS ====================
    print(f"\n{'='*80}")
    print(" GENERALIZATION ANALYSIS")
    print(f"{'='*80}\n")

    mean_mimic_auc = np.mean(mimic_aucs)
    mean_chexpert_auc = np.mean(chexpert_aucs)
    gap = mean_chexpert_auc - mean_mimic_auc
    gap_pct = (gap / mean_mimic_auc) * 100

    print(f"Internal AUC (MIMIC):    {mean_mimic_auc:.4f}")
    print(f"External AUC (CheXpert): {mean_chexpert_auc:.4f}")
    print(f"Performance Gap:         {gap:+.4f} ({gap_pct:+.1f}%)\n")

    # Interpret generalization
    if abs(gap_pct) < 10:
        status = "Excellent generalization (gap < 10%)"
    elif abs(gap_pct) < 20:
        status = "Good generalization (gap < 20%)"
    else:
        status = "Moderate generalization gap"

    print(f"Status: {status}\n")

    # ==================== SAVE RESULTS ====================
    results = {
        'architecture': architecture,
        'mimic_test': {
            'mean_auc': float(mean_mimic_auc),
            'mean_auprc': float(np.mean(mimic_auprcs)),
            'mean_f1': float(np.mean(mimic_f1s)),
            'per_pathology': {
                k: {
                    kk: float(vv) if isinstance(vv, (np.floating, float)) else int(vv)
                    for kk, vv in v.items()
                }
                for k, v in mimic_metrics.items()
            }
        },
        'chexpert': {
            'mean_auc': float(mean_chexpert_auc),
            'mean_auprc': float(np.mean(chexpert_auprcs)),
            'mean_f1': float(np.mean(chexpert_f1s)),
            'per_pathology': {
                k: {
                    kk: float(vv) if isinstance(vv, (np.floating, float)) else int(vv)
                    for kk, vv in v.items()
                }
                for k, v in chexpert_metrics.items()
            }
        },
        'generalization': {
            'internal_auc': float(mean_mimic_auc),
            'external_auc': float(mean_chexpert_auc),
            'gap': float(gap),
            'gap_percent': float(gap_pct),
            'status': status
        }
    }

    # Save to JSON
    results_path = Config.RESULTS_DIR / f'{architecture}_results.json'
    with open(results_path, 'w') as f:
        json.dump(results, f, indent=2)

    print(f" Results saved: {results_path}\n")

    return results

print(" Cross-institutional validation function defined")
print("  - Evaluates on MIMIC-CXR (internal)")
print("  - Evaluates on CheXpert (external)")
print("  - Computes generalization gap\n")

 Cross-institutional validation function defined
  - Evaluates on MIMIC-CXR (internal)
  - Evaluates on CheXpert (external)
  - Computes generalization gap

"""
CHUNK 14: Create dataloaders (Direct from Google Drive)
"""

print("=" * 70)
print("CREATING DATALOADERS (from Google Drive)")
print("=" * 70)

# Create split CSVs in Drive
mimic_df = pd.read_csv("/content/drive/MyDrive/chest-xray-project/datasets/mimic-cxr/mimic_subset_50k.csv")
mimic_df[mimic_df['split'] == 'train'].to_csv('/content/drive/MyDrive/chest-xray-project/datasets/mimic_train.csv', index=False)
mimic_df[mimic_df['split'] == 'validate'].to_csv('/content/drive/MyDrive/chest-xray-project/datasets/mimic_val.csv', index=False)
mimic_df[mimic_df['split'] == 'test'].to_csv('/content/drive/MyDrive/chest-xray-project/datasets/mimic_test.csv', index=False)

print("CSVs created")

# Use num_workers=2 (compromise between speed and stability)
train_loader = DataLoader(
    ChestXRayDataset('/content/drive/MyDrive/chest-xray-project/datasets/mimic_train.csv',
                     '/content/drive/MyDrive/chest-xray-project/datasets/mimic-cxr/files',
                     transform=get_train_transforms()),
    batch_size=Config.BATCH_SIZE, shuffle=True, num_workers=2, pin_memory=True
)

val_loader = DataLoader(
    ChestXRayDataset('/content/drive/MyDrive/chest-xray-project/datasets/mimic_val.csv',
                     '/content/drive/MyDrive/chest-xray-project/datasets/mimic-cxr/files',
                     transform=get_val_transforms()),
    batch_size=Config.BATCH_SIZE, shuffle=False, num_workers=2, pin_memory=True
)

test_loader = DataLoader(
    ChestXRayDataset('/content/drive/MyDrive/chest-xray-project/datasets/mimic_test.csv',
                     '/content/drive/MyDrive/chest-xray-project/datasets/mimic-cxr/files',
                     transform=get_val_transforms()),
    batch_size=Config.BATCH_SIZE, shuffle=False, num_workers=2, pin_memory=True
)

chexpert_loader = DataLoader(
    ChestXRayDataset('/content/drive/MyDrive/chest-xray-project/datasets/chexpert/valid.csv',
                     '/content/drive/MyDrive/chest-xray-project/datasets/chexpert/valid',
                     transform=get_val_transforms()),
    batch_size=Config.BATCH_SIZE, shuffle=False, num_workers=2, pin_memory=True
)

print(f" Train: {len(train_loader.dataset)} images")
print(f" Val: {len(val_loader.dataset)} images")
print(f" Test: {len(test_loader.dataset)} images")
print(f" CheXpert: {len(chexpert_loader.dataset)} images")
print("\n DATALOADERS READY")

# Load pos_weights
pos_weights = torch.load(Config.OUTPUT_DIR / 'pos_weights.pt')
print(f" pos_weights loaded")

# Train EfficientNet-B0
efficientnet_model, efficientnet_history = train_model(
    architecture='efficientnet_b0',
    train_loader=train_loader,
    val_loader=val_loader,
    device=device,
    pos_weights=pos_weights
)

efficientnet_results = cross_institutional_validation(
    model=efficientnet_model,
    architecture='efficientnet_b0',
    test_loader=test_loader,
    chexpert_loader=chexpert_loader,
    device=device
)

print("\n EfficientNet-B0 complete!")

"""
CHUNK 16: Train DenseNet-121
"""

print("\n\n")
print("#"*80)
print("# ARCHITECTURE 1/2: DENSENET-121")
print("#"*80)
print()

# Train DenseNet-121
densenet_model, densenet_history = train_model(
    architecture='densenet121',
    train_loader=train_loader,
    val_loader=val_loader,
    device=device,
    pos_weights=pos_weights
)

# Evaluate DenseNet-121
densenet_results = cross_institutional_validation(
    model=densenet_model,
    architecture='densenet121',
    test_loader=test_loader,
    chexpert_loader=chexpert_loader,
    device=device
)

# Free GPU memory
del densenet_model
torch.cuda.empty_cache()

print("\n DenseNet-121 training and evaluation complete!\n")

# Recreate CheXpert loader with fixed class
chexpert_loader = DataLoader(
    ChestXRayDataset('/content/drive/MyDrive/chest-xray-project/datasets/chexpert/valid.csv',
                     '/content/drive/MyDrive/chest-xray-project/datasets/chexpert/valid',
                     transform=get_val_transforms()),
    batch_size=Config.BATCH_SIZE, shuffle=False, num_workers=Config.NUM_WORKERS, pin_memory=True
)

# Re-load model and evaluate
densenet_model = ChestXRayClassifier(architecture='densenet121', num_classes=Config.NUM_CLASSES, pretrained=False)
densenet_model.load_state_dict(torch.load(Config.MODELS_DIR / 'densenet121_best.pth'))
densenet_model = densenet_model.to(device)

densenet_results = cross_institutional_validation(
    model=densenet_model,
    architecture='densenet121',
    test_loader=test_loader,
    chexpert_loader=chexpert_loader,
    device=device
)

del densenet_model
torch.cuda.empty_cache()

"""
CHUNK 18: Final Summary and Save Combined Results
"""

print("\n\n")
print("="*80)
print(" ALL TRAINING COMPLETED SUCCESSFULLY!")
print("="*80)
print()

# Combine results
all_results = {
    'densenet121': densenet_results,
    'efficientnet_b0': efficientnet_results
}

# Save combined results
combined_results_path = Config.RESULTS_DIR / 'densenet_efficientnet_results.json'
with open(combined_results_path, 'w') as f:
    json.dump(all_results, f, indent=2)

print(f" Combined results saved: {combined_results_path}\n")

# ==================== FINAL SUMMARY TABLE ====================
print("="*80)
print(" FINAL PERFORMANCE SUMMARY")
print("="*80)
print()

print(f"{'Architecture':<20s} {'Internal AUC':>15s} {'External AUC':>15s} {'Gap':>10s} {'Status':<30s}")
print("-"*80)

for arch, res in all_results.items():
    internal_auc = res['generalization']['internal_auc']
    external_auc = res['generalization']['external_auc']
    gap_pct = res['generalization']['gap_percent']
    status = res['generalization']['status']

    print(f"{arch.upper():<20s} {internal_auc:15.4f} {external_auc:15.4f} {gap_pct:>9.1f}% {status:<30s}")

print()
print("="*80)
print()

# Print file locations
print("All outputs saved to:")
print(f"   Models:  {Config.MODELS_DIR}")
print(f"   Results: {Config.RESULTS_DIR}")
print(f"   Figures: {Config.FIGURES_DIR}")
print()

print("Model files:")
print(f"   densenet121_best.pth")
print(f"   efficientnet_b0_best.pth")
print()

print("Result files:")
print(f"   densenet121_results.json")
print(f"   efficientnet_b0_results.json")
print(f"   densenet_efficientnet_results.json")
print()

print(f"   densenet121_training_curves.png")
print(f"   efficientnet_b0_training_curves.png")
